```python
import pandas as pd
from collections import Counter
```

### Step-by-step Instructions:

Step 1: Create a DataFrame for storing user reviews.

```python
user_reviews = {
    'Product': ['Caudalie Favorites', 'No Brainer Gentle Facial Cleanser', 
                'LANGE HAIR Extendé Conditioning Detangler Hair Spray',
                'Vinosource SOS Intense Hydration Set', 'Karuna 7 Days of Glow', 
                'STARAMZ 7 Set Bachelorette Scrunchies', 'NIRA Skincare Laser & Serum Bundle'], 
    'Description': [
        "I am a big fan of caudalie products.", 
        "It smells amazing. It has a thicker consistency", 
        "Has a great smell but I found the product", 
        "All the products are high quality", 
        "After the week my skin did feel very well hydrated",
        "These would be great in a proposal box", 
        "Occasionally I would get a little “zap’"]
}
df_user_reviews = pd.DataFrame(user_reviews).set_index('Product')
print(df_user_reviews['Description'])
```
Step 2: Count word frequencies across reviews.

```python
word_freq = df_user_reviews['Description'].apply(lambda x: str(x.lower()).split())
for i, row in enumerate(word_freq):
    print(f"Review {i+1} Word Frequencies:")
    print(Counter(row))
```
Step 3: Identify top keywords reflecting user preferences.

```python
top_keywords = []
for freq_dist in word_freq.values.tolist():
    if not isinstance(freq_dist[0], dict): # Skip empty reviews
        continue
    top_keyword = max(set([k for k, v in freq_dist]), key=lambda x: sum(v.count(w)/len(v) for w in [x]))
    top_keywords.append(top_keyword)
print("Top Keywords:", ', '.join(map(str.upper, set(top_keywords))))
```
Step 4: Synthesize insights into user preferences.

```python
# Print Overall Insights
print("\nUser Preference Insights:")
if len(set(top_keywords)) == 1:
    preferred_brand_name = f"'{next(iter(top_keywords))}'"
else:
    preferred_brands_names = map(str.title, set(top_keywords))
    preferred_brand_name = "'or'.join(preferred_brands_names)"
print(f"The user seems interested in '{preferred_brand_name}'.")
print("Additional observations...")
```
